have the option to enter in this transaction; the short party will, at the option of\n    59→   * the long party, potentially enter into the inverse transaction.\n    60→   */\n    61→  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n    62→  private final LongShort longShort;\n    63→  /**\n    64→   * The expiry date of the option.\n    65→   * <p>\n    66→   * The option is European, always be positive\n   129→   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   130→   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   131→   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   132→   */\n   133→  public static FxVanillaOption of(\n   134→      LongShort longShort,\n   135→      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n   136→      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n   137→      PutCall putCall,\n   138→      double strike,\n   139→      double baseNotional,\n   140→      LocalDate paymentDate,\n   141→      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n   142→\n   143→    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n   144→    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n   145→\n   146→    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n   147→    // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n   148→    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n   149→    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n   150→    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n   151→    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n   152→    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n   153→    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n   154→        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   */\n  public static FxVanillaOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n
